      * { animation-duration: 0.01ms !important; animation-iteration-count: 1 !important; transition-duration: 0.01ms !important; }
    }

  <script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
    (function() {
      // ===== PARTÍCULAS =====
      if (!window.matchMedia('(prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)').matches) {
        const cvs = document.querySelector('.wlf__particles');
        if (cvs) {
          const ctx = cvs.getContext('2d');
          let W, H, particles = [];

          function resizeCanvas() {
            W = cvs.clientWidth; H = cvs.clientHeight;
            cvs.width = W; cvs.height = H;
            initParticles();
          }
          function initParticles() {
            particles = Array.from({ length: 18 }, () => ({
              x: Math.random() * W, y: Math.random() * H,
              r: Math.random() * 1.6 + 0.4,
              vx: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.2,
              vy: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.2,
              a: Math.random() * 0.4 + 0.2
            }));
          }
          function drawParticles() {
            ctx.clearRect(0, 0, W, H);
            for (const p of particles) {
              p.x += p.vx; p.y += p.vy;
              if (p.x < -10) p.x = W + 10; if (p.x > W + 10) p.x = -10;
              if (p.y < -10) p.y = H + 10; if (p.y > H + 10) p.y = -10;
              ctx.beginPath();
              ctx.arc(p.x, p.y, p.r, 0, Math.PI * 2);
              ctx.fillStyle = `rgba(255,46,46,${p.a})`;
              ctx.fill();
            }
            requestAnimationFrame(drawParticles);
          }
          let resizeTimer;
          window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
            clearTimeout(resizeTimer);
            resizeTimer = setTimeout(resizeCanvas, 100);
          }, { passive: true });
          resizeCanvas(); drawParticles();
        }
      }

      // ===== DIAL =====
      const coin = document.getElementById('coin');
      if (!coin) return;

      const container = coin.parentElement;
      const quoteEl   = document.getElementById('quote');

      const bands = [
        { t: 0.05, q: 'Nada é de graça.',              v: 0  },
        { t: 0.15, q: 'Tempo não negocia perdão.',      v: 1  },
        { t: 0.25, q: 'Cada segundo é uma decisão.',    v: 2  },
        { t: 0.35, q: 'Ambição devora os fracos.',      v: 3  },
        { t: 0.45, q: 'Ganância é fome eterna.',        v: 4  },
        { t: 0.55, q: 'Toda conquista tem um preço.',   v: 5  },
        { t: 0.65, q: 'O trono exige sacrifícios.',     v: 6  },
        { t: 0.75, q: 'Poder é vício sem cura.',        v: 7  },
        { t: 0.85, q: 'Uma coroa pesa em muitas almas.',v: 8  },
        { t: 0.95, q: 'Domínio tem preço de sangue.',   v: 9  },
        { t: 1.01, q: 'Poder cobra juros altos.',       v: 10 }
      ];

      let isDragging = false;
      let coinSize   = 64;
      let spinY      = 0;
      let lastBand   = -1;
      let currentPercent = 0.5;

      function setQuote(bandIndex) {
        if (bandIndex === lastBand) return;
        lastBand = bandIndex;
        const newQuote = bands[Math.max(0, bandIndex)].q;
        if (quoteEl.textContent === newQuote) return;
        quoteEl.style.opacity   = '0';
        quoteEl.style.transform = 'translateY(-6px)';
        setTimeout(() => {
          quoteEl.textContent     = newQuote;
          quoteEl.style.opacity   = '1';
          quoteEl.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
        }, 120);
        coin.setAttribute('aria-valuenow', bands[Math.max(0, bandIndex)].v);
      }

      function updatePosition(clientX) {
        const rect  = container.getBoundingClientRect();
        const maxDx = Math.max(1, rect.width - coinSize);
        let dx      = clientX - rect.left - coinSize / 2;
        dx          = Math.max(0, Math.min(dx, maxDx));
        currentPercent = dx / maxDx;

        coin.style.setProperty('--dx',   dx + 'px');
        coin.style.setProperty('--tilt', ((currentPercent - 0.5) * 20) + 'deg');

        const bandIndex = bands.findIndex(b => currentPercent < b.t);
        setQuote(bandIndex);
      }

      function spinCoin() {
        spinY += 360;
        coin.style.setProperty('--spinY', spinY + 'deg');
        coin.style.transition = 'transform 600ms cubic-bezier(0.2, 0.8, 0.2, 1)';
        setTimeout(() => { coin.style.transition = 'none'; }, 620);
      }

      function centerCoin() {
        recalcCoinSize();
        const rect  = container.getBoundingClientRect();
        const maxDx = Math.max(1, rect.width - coinSize);
        coin.style.setProperty('--dx',   (maxDx / 2) + 'px');
        coin.style.setProperty('--tilt', '0deg');
        coin.setAttribute('aria-valuenow', '5');
        lastBand = -1;
        currentPercent = 0.5;
      }

      function recalcCoinSize() { coinSize = coin.offsetWidth || 64; }

      // ── Interação por teclado (requisito ARIA slider) ──
      coin.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
        const step = 1 / bands.length;
        let changed = false;
        if (e.key === 'ArrowRight' || e.key === 'ArrowUp') {
          currentPercent = Math.min(1, currentPercent + step);
          changed = true;
        } else if (e.key === 'ArrowLeft' || e.key === 'ArrowDown') {
          currentPercent = Math.max(0, currentPercent - step);
          changed = true;
        } else if (e.key === 'Home') {
          currentPercent = 0; changed = true;
        } else if (e.key === 'End') {
          currentPercent = 1; changed = true;
        }
        if (!changed) return;
        e.preventDefault();
        recalcCoinSize();
        const rect  = container.getBoundingClientRect();
        const maxDx = Math.max(1, rect.width - coinSize);
        const dx    = currentPercent * maxDx;
        coin.style.setProperty('--dx',   dx + 'px');
        coin.style.setProperty('--tilt', ((currentPercent - 0.5) * 20) + 'deg');
        const bandIndex = bands.findIndex(b => currentPercent < b.t);
        setQuote(bandIndex);
      });

      // ── Ponteiros / toque ──
      function onPointerDown(e) {
        isDragging = true;
        recalcCoinSize();
        spinCoin();
        const x = e.clientX ?? e.touches?.[0]?.clientX;
        if (typeof x === 'number') updatePosition(x);
        e.preventDefault();
      }
      function onPointerMove(e) {
        if (!isDragging) return;
        const x = e.clientX ?? e.touches?.[0]?.clientX;
        if (typeof x === 'number') requestAnimationFrame(() => updatePosition(x));
        e.preventDefault();
      }
      function onPointerUp() { isDragging = false; }

      if (window.PointerEvent) {
        coin.addEventListener('pointerdown',   onPointerDown, { passive: false });
        window.addEventListener('pointermove', onPointerMove, { passive: false });
        window.addEventListener('pointerup',   onPointerUp,   { passive: true  });
        window.addEventListener('pointercancel', onPointerUp, { passive: true  });
      } else {
        coin.addEventListener('mousedown',       onPointerDown);
        window.addEventListener('mousemove',     onPointerMove);
        window.addEventListener('mouseup',       onPointerUp);
        coin.addEventListener('touchstart',      onPointerDown, { passive: false });
        window.addEventListener('touchmove',     onPointerMove, { passive: false });
        window.addEventListener('touchend',      onPointerUp,   { passive: true });
      }

      let resizeTimeout;
      window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
        clearTimeout(resizeTimeout);
        resizeTimeout = setTimeout(centerCoin, 100);
      }, { passive: true });

      setTimeout(centerCoin, 50);
    })();
  </script>

<template id="tp-language" data-tp-language="pt_BR"></template><script type="speculationrules">
{"prefetch":[{"source":"document","where":{"and":[{"href_matches":"/*"},{"not":{"href_matches":["/wp-*.php","/wp-admin/*","/wp-content/uploads/*","/wp-content/*","/wp-content/plugins/*","/wp-content/themes/hello-elementor/*","/*\\?(.+)"]}},{"not":{"selector_matches":"a[rel~=\"nofollow\"]"}},{"not":{"selector_matches":".no-prefetch, .no-prefetch a"}}]},"eagerness":"conservative"}]}
</script>
  <script type="rocketlazyloadscript">
    (function(){
      const btn  = document.querySelector('.wg-burger');
      const pane = document.getElementById('wg-menu-panel');
      const ovl  = document.querySelector('.wg-backdrop');
      if(!pane) return;

      const mq = window.matchMedia('(min-width: 961px)');
      let lastFocus = null;

      function lockScroll(on){
        document.documentElement.classList.toggle('wg-lock', on);
        document.body.classList.toggle('wg-lock', on);
      }

      function syncPane(){
        if(mq.matches){
          pane.hidden = false;
          pane.removeAttribute('data-open');
          btn && btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false');
          ovl && ovl.removeAttribute('data-show');
          lockScroll(false);
          pane.querySelectorAll('.sub-menu').forEach(ul => ul.removeAttribute('data-open'));
          pane.querySelectorAll(':scope > ul.wg-menu > li.menu-item-has-children > a[aria-expanded]').forEach(a=>{
            a.removeAttribute('aria-expanded'); a.removeAttribute('aria-controls');
          });
        }else{
          if(!pane.hasAttribute('data-open')) pane.hidden = true;
          prepareMobileSubmenus();
        }
      }

      function firstFocusable(root){
        return root.querySelector('a,button,[tabindex]:not([tabindex="-1"])');
      }

      function openMenu(){
        lastFocus = document.activeElement;
        pane.hidden = false;
        pane.setAttribute('data-open','true');
        btn && btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true');
        ovl && ovl.setAttribute('data-show','true');
        lockScroll(true);
        const f = firstFocusable(pane); f && f.focus();
      }
      function closeMenu(){
        pane.removeAttribute('data-open');
        btn && btn.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false');
        ovl && ovl.removeAttribute('data-show');
        lockScroll(false);
        setTimeout(()=>{ if(!mq.matches && !pane.hasAttribute('data-open')) pane.hidden = true; }, 200);
        lastFocus && lastFocus.focus();
      }

      btn && btn.addEventListener('click', ()=>{ (pane.getAttribute('data-open')==='true') ? closeMenu() : openMenu(); });

      document.addEventListener('keydown', (e)=>{
        if(e.key === 'Escape') closeMenu();
        if(e.key === 'Tab' && pane.getAttribute('data-open')==='true' && !mq.matches){
          const focusables = pane.querySelectorAll('a,button,[tabindex]:not([tabindex="-1"])');
          const list = Array.from(focusables).filter(el=>!el.hasAttribute('disabled'));
          if (!list.length) return;
          const first = list[0], last = list[list.length-1];
          if (e.shiftKey && document.activeElement===first){ e.preventDefault(); last.focus(); }
          else if (!e.shiftKey && document.activeElement===last){ e.preventDefault(); first.focus(); }
        }
      });

      document.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
        if(!mq.matches && !pane.contains(e.target) && !btn?.contains(e.target)) closeMenu();
        if(ovl && e.target === ovl) closeMenu();
      });

      mq.addEventListener?.('change', syncPane);

      function prepareMobileSubmenus(){
        pane.querySelectorAll(':scope > ul.wg-menu > li.menu-item-has-children').forEach((li, idx) => {
          const a = li.querySelector(':scope > a');
          const sub = li.querySelector(':scope > .sub-menu');
          if(!a || !sub) return;

          const id = sub.id || ('wg-sub-' + idx + '-' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2,7));
          sub.id = id;

          sub.removeAttribute('data-open');
          a.setAttribute('aria-controls', id);
          a.setAttribute('aria-expanded', 'false');

          function toggleSub(e){
            e.preventDefault();
            const isOpen = sub.getAttribute('data-open') === 'true';
            li.parentElement.querySelectorAll(':scope > li.menu-item-has-children > .sub-menu[data-open="true"]').forEach(other => {
              if(other !== sub){
                other.removeAttribute('data-open');
                const ao = other.parentElement.querySelector(':scope > a[aria-expanded]');
                ao && ao.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false');
              }
            });
            if(isOpen){
              sub.removeAttribute('data-open');
              a.setAttribute('aria-expanded','false');
            }else{
              sub.setAttribute('data-open','true');
              a.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true');
              sub.scrollIntoView({block:'nearest'});
            }
          }
          if(!a.dataset.wgBound){
            a.addEventListener('click', toggleSub);
            a.addEventListener('keydown', (ev)=>{ if(ev.key==='Enter' || ev.key===' '){ toggleSub(ev); } });
            a.dataset.wgBound = '1';
          }
        });
      }

      syncPane();

      /* v1.6: ativa efeitos visuais (blur) só após ocioso/LCP */
      (function enableNavFx(){
        const on = ()=> document.documentElement.classList.add('wg-ready');
        if ('requestIdleCallback' in window) {
          requestIdleCallback(on, {timeout: 1200});
        } else {
          window.addEventListener('load', ()=> setTimeout(on, 300));
        }
      })();
    })();
  </script>

<script type="rocketlazyloadscript" id="cmplz-cookiebanner-js-after">window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
		if ('undefined' != typeof window.jQuery) {
			jQuery(document).ready(function ($) {
				$(document).on('elementor/popup/show', () => {
					let rev_cats = cmplz_categories.reverse();
					for (let key in rev_cats) {
						if (rev_cats.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
							let category = cmplz_categories[key];
							if (cmplz_has_consent(category)) {
								document.querySelectorAll('[data-category="' + category + '"]').forEach(obj => {
									cmplz_remove_placeholder(obj);
								});
							}
						}
					}

					let services = cmplz_get_services_on_page();
					for (let key in services) {
						if (services.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
							let service = services[key].service;
							let category = services[key].category;
							if (cmplz_has_service_consent(service, category)) {
								document.querySelectorAll('[data-service="' + service + '"]').forEach(obj => {
									cmplz_remove_placeholder(obj);
								});
							}
						}
					}
				});
			});
		}
    
    
		
			document.addEventListener("cmplz_enable_category", function(consentData) {
				var category = consentData.detail.category;
				var services = consentData.detail.services;
				var blockedContentContainers = [];
				let selectorVideo = '.cmplz-elementor-widget-video-playlist[data-category="'+category+'"],.elementor-widget-video[data-category="'+category+'"]';
				let selectorGeneric = '[data-cmplz-elementor-href][data-category="'+category+'"]';
				for (var skey in services) {
					if (services.hasOwnProperty(skey)) {
						let service = skey;
						selectorVideo +=',.cmplz-elementor-widget-video-playlist[data-service="'+service+'"],.elementor-widget-video[data-service="'+service+'"]';
						selectorGeneric +=',[data-cmplz-elementor-href][data-service="'+service+'"]';
					}
				}
				document.querySelectorAll(selectorVideo).forEach(obj => {
					let elementService = obj.getAttribute('data-service');
					if ( cmplz_is_service_denied(elementService) ) {
						return;
					}
					if (obj.classList.contains('cmplz-elementor-activated')) return;
					obj.classList.add('cmplz-elementor-activated');

					if ( obj.hasAttribute('data-cmplz_elementor_widget_type') ){
						let attr = obj.getAttribute('data-cmplz_elementor_widget_type');
						obj.classList.removeAttribute('data-cmplz_elementor_widget_type');
						obj.classList.setAttribute('data-widget_type', attr);
					}
					if (obj.classList.contains('cmplz-elementor-widget-video-playlist')) {
						obj.classList.remove('cmplz-elementor-widget-video-playlist');
						obj.classList.add('elementor-widget-video-playlist');
					}
					obj.setAttribute('data-settings', obj.getAttribute('data-cmplz-elementor-settings'));
					blockedContentContainers.push(obj);
				});

				document.querySelectorAll(selectorGeneric).forEach(obj => {
					let elementService = obj.getAttribute('data-service');
					if ( cmplz_is_service_denied(elementService) ) {
						return;
					}
					if (obj.classList.contains('cmplz-elementor-activated')) return;

					if (obj.classList.contains('cmplz-fb-video')) {
						obj.classList.remove('cmplz-fb-video');
						obj.classList.add('fb-video');
					}

					obj.classList.add('cmplz-elementor-activated');
					obj.setAttribute('data-href', obj.getAttribute('data-cmplz-elementor-href'));
					blockedContentContainers.push(obj.closest('.elementor-widget'));
				});

				/**
				 * Trigger the widgets in Elementor
				 */
				for (var key in blockedContentContainers) {
					if (blockedContentContainers.hasOwnProperty(key) && blockedContentContainers[key] !== undefined) {
						let blockedContentContainer = blockedContentContainers[key];
						if (elementorFrontend.elementsHandler) {
							elementorFrontend.elementsHandler.runReadyTrigger(blockedContentContainer)
						}
						var cssIndex = blockedContentContainer.getAttribute('data-placeholder_class_index');
						blockedContentContainer.classList.remove('cmplz-blocked-content-container');
						blockedContentContainer.classList.remove('cmplz-placeholder-' + cssIndex);
					}
				}

			});
		
		
        
            document.addEventListener("cmplz_enable_category", function () {
                document.querySelectorAll('[data-rocket-lazyload]').forEach(obj => {
                    if (obj.hasAttribute('data-lazy-src')) {
                        obj.setAttribute('src', obj.getAttribute('data-lazy-src'));
                    }
                });
            });
        
		

	let cmplzBlockedContent = document.querySelector('.cmplz-blocked-content-notice');
	if ( cmplzBlockedContent) {
	        cmplzBlockedContent.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
            event.stopPropagation();
        });
	}
